er qie yong hen jiu cai xu yao geng huan
suo yi fei jiu dian chi ru he chu li
wo hai zhen mei zhu yi
he xian sheng biao shi hui ba fei jiu dian chi he qi ta la ji yi qi fang dao tong yi ge dai zi li reng diao
dui yu sui yi diu qi fei jiu dian chi ke neng zao cheng de wei hai
he xian sheng biao shi bing bu liao jie
jia zhu tian he mou xiao qu de lin xiao jie zao zao jia ru
la ji fen lei de hang lie
wo hui ba chu yu la ji he sheng huo la ji fen kai dao
er dui yu fei jiu dian chi
lin xiao jie biao shi
mei you kan dao you zhuan men hui shou dian chi de di fang
zhi hao he sheng huo la ji yi qi reng diao
wo zhi dao jiu dian chi dui huan jing you hai
mai dao tu li hao xiang hui chan sheng gong wu ran
fei jiu dian chi wu chu ke reng ye rang ta gan dao hen wu nai
ji zhe zai lin xiao jie suo zai xiao qu zou fang fa xian
xiao qu nei duo chu she zhi le la ji fen lei de xuan chuan ban
qi zhong ti dao le dui bu tong lei bie la ji de jie ding
yi ji la ji hui chan sheng wei hai de jian dan jie shao
fei chong dian dian chi
fei kou zi dian chi deng nie ge dian chi yang hua gong dian chi bei hua fen dao you hai la ji fen lei
hai jian dan jie shao le
you hai la ji shi zhi cun zai dui ren ti jian kang you hai de zhong jin shu
you du de wu zhi huo zhe dui huan jing zao cheng xian shi wei hai
qian zai wei hai de fei qi wu
zai xiao qu de la ji fang li
ge qi ta la ji la ji tong
ge chu yu la ji la ji tong yi ji
ge you hai la ji la ji tong
er you hai la ji la ji tong nei zhuang man le deng guan
ji zhe zan wei kan dao you xiao qu ju min qi zhi de jiu dian chi
er zai xiao qu de zui li ce
she zhi le yi ge fen lei la ji tong
bao kuo jiu yi wu hui shou xiang
zhi he hui shou xiang
guo qi yao pin he fei dian chi hui shou xiang
dan ji zhe fa xian
guo qi yao pin de tou fang kou ke yi da kai fang zhi guo qi yao pin
er fei dian chi de tou fang kou ze bu zhi he gu wu fa da kai
zhu zai tong yi xiao qu de li nv shi biao shi
ping shi you zhu yi dao xiao qu de fen lei la ji xiang
shang yi ci reng dian chi shi qu nian nian di
te yi na guo qu reng
dian chi hui shou xiang
xiao qu li mian zuo guo la ji fen lei de xuan chuan
zhi dao sui yi luan reng dian chi de wei hai hen da
ye hui gao su hai zi yao jin xing la ji fen lei
dan chong dian bao ne
ye ke yi reng zai fei jiu dian chi de hui shou xiang li ma
lin xiao jie kan zhe chou ti li die cheng yi dui de chong dian bao fa chu yi wen
lin xiao jie hai xiang zhi dao
zai zi ji zuo wan la ji fen lei hou
zhe xie la ji dou hui ru he jin xing chu li
jiu xiang fei jiu dian chi
zai ji zhong hui shou hou hui zen me chu li
shi bu shi zhen de mei you wei hai le
dou shi shei zai chu li
zhi dao zi ji zai zuo de shi qing you shen me yi yi hen zhong yao
ru guo zhi dao fei jiu dian chi de ji zhong hui shou chu li que shi you xiao guo
wo xiang hui you geng duo ren jia ru fen lei hui shou de dui wu
jia zhong bu shao chang suo dou li bu kai yi jie xiao xiao de dian chi
mei nian yong xia lai
ye hui chan sheng yi dui fei dian chi
you shi min nai xin di shou ji hao
zui zhong yi qi reng dao you hai la ji fen lei la ji tong li
nan dao bu shi you hai la ji ma
shi shi shang hai zhen bu yi ding shi
yue xiu qu cheng shi guan li ju fen lei guan li ban gong shi zhu ren chen xiao long jie shao

shi yi ci xing de

chen xiao long biao shi
ru guo shi min reng an zhao chuan tong de si wei jiang gan dian chi tou fang zai you hai la ji de la ji tong li

huo shi gen sui you hai la ji bei shou yun dao lin shi chu cun dian
dan zui hou song dao chu li chang shi

yi yue xiu qu wei li

na mi lv se yin shua de he xin li nian jiu shi jiang na mi cai liao he yin shua ji shu xiang jie he

bing xing cheng le bao kuo

wo men lai dao le wei yu yi se lie bei bu zui da de xue yuan xing yi yuan rui ben yi liao zhong xin
rui ben yi liao zhong xin shi shi jie zhi ming de shi fan jiao xue yi yuan he chuang xin zhong xin
ta zhi suo yi neng gou cheng wei chuang xin zhong xin
gen zhe zuo yi yuan de qu wei po you guan xi
rui ben yi liao zhong xin he bei yu wei
yi se lie ma sheng li gong
de yi se lie li gong xue yuan de fu shu ji gou
lu si he bu lu si la pa bo te yi xue yuan
la pa bo te jia zu yi xue ke xue yan jiu suo zuo luo yu tong yi xiao qu
yi yuan ye you zi ji de yan fa zhong xin
mu qian zheng zai jian she yi dong geng da de yan fa zhong xin
yi xue yuan tong guo yu chan ye he zuo
lin chuang yi xue jie he
gong tong wei yi xue ke xue gong xian le fa zhan dong li
yi se lie li gong xue yuan la pa bo te jia zu yi xue ke xue yan jiu suo te pin jiao shou
nuo bei er hua xue jiang de zhu a long
qie ha nuo wo jiao shou zheng shi zai zhe li wan cheng le ta de ke xue yan jiu
ta gao su ji zhe
yi se lie li gong da xue yi xue yuan yu zhu xiao qu fen ge kai
er yu yi yuan jin jin xiang lian

rui ben yi liao zhong xin chuang jian yu

ji ke jiao yan xue yu yi ti

zai zhe ge yi yuan zhong
chu le chuang shang zhi liao zhong xin
xin xue guan yi yuan
zhong liu zhi liao zhong xin
er tong yi yuan deng lian pian de yi liao qu
zui ling ren jing tan de jiu shi wei yu di xia ting che chang de ying ji yi yuan
ao fu er fang yu di xia ying ji yi yuan
cheng zuo dian ti lai dao yi yuan de di xia ceng
zhe li bu guo shi pu tong de di xia ting che chang
ran er da kai che wei hou fang de juan zha men
yi ge xian dai hua de ji jiu shi li ke ying ru yan lian
zhe zuo ke rong na
liang che de san ceng di xia ting che chang
zai zhan zheng shi qi huo zhe tu fa zhong da qing kuang shi
xiao shi nei zheng ti
cheng wei she shi wan bei
zhang bing chuang de zhan di yi yuan
shi quan qiu zui da de di xia ying ji xi tong
yi yuan de qiang shang lian jie zhe ge zhong she bei
pei zhi le quan tao de shui

sui ran yi yuan yi gong zhi you
dan ji jiu zhong xin que an zhao
zhang chuang wei de gui mo jian she
zhang chuang wei ke man zu dang di
jia da yi yuan de xu qiu
ba yan er jie shao
gao xiao he yan jiu zhong xin
hai you hen duo chuang xin qi ye zuo luo zai zhe ge yi liao zhong xin suo zai pian qu
ta men ye hui he zhe xie chuang xin qi ye he zuo
ta men dou hui tong guo ke yan xiang mu jin xing duo fang he zuo
ta men ye fei chang xu yao tong guo chuang xin gong si dui ji shu jin xing chan ye zhuan hua
ba yan er ceng liang ci dao guang zhou de yi yuan jin xing kao cha
guang zhou zai hen duo ling yu de yi liao ji shu dou shi fen ling xian
ta ye qi dai zai xin yao kai fa
yi liao she bei yan fa deng ling yu yu guang zhou zhan kai he zuo

nian chu sheng zai yi se lie hai fa

hou dao ma sheng li gong xue yuan cong shi bo shi hou yan jiu
ta suo zai de ke yan tuan dui tu po xing de fa xian le ren lei xi bao ru he kong zhi mou zhong dan bai zhi di guo cheng

yi zhong dan bai zhi jiang jie de zhong yao ji li

nin shi qi zhong yi wei
zuo wei yi ming ke xue jia
nin ren wei yi se lie gei le nin zen yang de chuang xin huan jing
sui ran yi se lie shi yi ge nian qing de guo jia
dan wo men cong chuan tong zhong xing cheng le re ai xue shu de wen hua
wo de fu qin zai wo bu dao

you qi shi sheng wu yi yao

da xue de zuo yong
xiang zai yi se lie

zhe xie chuang xin zhe men yi bei zi dou mei you shang guo da xue

sui huo gao zhong bi ye hou jiu yao fu bing yi

wo ren wei wo xian zai hai mei you da an

zhe shi yi ge shi yan
wo bu neng bao zheng jie guo

mao gong bu ci zhang su ge

su ge bo shi kan kan er tan
ta xiang yi wei xiang dao yi ban jie shi

yi sheng wu yi yao
chuang ye tou zi wei zhong dian

ta ju you de chao qiang yin li shi de guang ye wu fa tao tuo ta de shi li fan wei
gai shi li fan wei cheng zuo hei dong de ban jing huo cheng zuo shi jian shi jie
hei dong zen me xing cheng de
xiang yu zhou wan wu yi yang
heng xing ye hui shuai lao si wang
yi xie da zhi liang heng xing zai he ju bian fan ying ran liao hao jin shi
nei he hui ji ju ta suo
suo you wu zhi kuai su xiang zhe yi ge dian tan suo
zui zhong tan suo cheng yi ke huang dou da xiao de qi dian
bing xing cheng yi ge qiang da de li chang xuan wo
niu qu zhou wei shi kong
tian wen xue jia jiang yu zhou zhong de hei dong fen cheng san lei
heng xing ji zhi liang hei dong
ji shi bei dao shang bai bei tai yang zhi liang
chao da zhi liang hei dong
ji bai wan bei tai yang zhi liang yi shang
he zhong deng zhi liang hei dong
jie yu liang zhe zhi jian
gen ju li lun tui suan
yin he xi zhong ying gai cun zai zhe shang qian wan ge heng xing liang ji de hei dong
yin wei hei dong zi shen bu fa she he fan she dian ci bo
yi qi he rou yan dou wu fa zhi jie guan ce dao ta
zen me zhi dao ta cun zai ne
tian wen xue jia men zhu yao shi tong guo ge zhong jian jie di zheng ju
qi ti de yun dong tou lu le hei dong de zong ji
hei dong you qiang yin li
dui zhou wei de heng xing
qi ti hui chan sheng ying xiang
ke yi tong guo guan ce zhe zhong ying xiang lai que ren hei dong de cun zai
er shi gen ju hei dong xi ji wu zhi
shi fa chu de guang lai pan duan hei dong de cun zai
di san ze shi tong guo kan dao hei dong cheng zhang de guo cheng
dao mu qian wei zhi
tong guo jian jie de guan ce
ke xue jia men zai yin he xi fa xian he que ren le

dan ke neng you shang qian wan ge heng xing ji hei dong hou xuan ti
zhong guo ke xue yuan shang hai tian wen tai yan jiu yuan shen zhi qiang shuo
yu zhou mei ge xing xi zhong xin dou you yi ge chao da zhi liang de hei dong
wo men ju zhu de yin he xi zhong xin jiu you yi ke
ta de zhi liang da yue shi tai yang zhi liang de

hei dong he yu zhou de dan sheng he yan hua you he guan xi
you he wo men ren lei you shen me guan xi
wei le geng zhun que qing xi de jie da zhe xie wen ti
ke xue jia men xiang zhi jie
guang yi xiang dui lun yu yan
sui ran hei dong ben shen bu fa guang
dan yin wei hei dong de cun zai
zhou wei shi kong wan qu
qi ti bei xi yin xia luo

yin li neng zhuan hua wei guang he re
yin ci qi ti bei jia re zhi shu shi yi she shi du
hei dong jiu xiang chen jin zai yi pian lei si fa guang qi ti de ming liang qu yu nei
shi jian shi jie kan qi lai jiu xiang yin ying
yin ying zhou wei huan rao zhe yi ge you xi ji huo pen liu fu she zao cheng de ru xin yue zhuang de guang huan
zhong guo ke xue yuan shang hai tian wen tai yan jiu yuan lu ru sen shuo
dui hei dong yin ying de cheng xiang jiang neng ti gong hei dong cun zai de zhi jie
zhe jiu bi xu yao bao zheng wang yuan jing zu gou ling min
neng fen bian de xi jie zu gou xiao
cong er bao zheng kan de dao he kan de qing
dan man zu shang shu suo you tiao jian
wang yuan jing de kou jing xu yao xiang di qiu da xiao
mu qian di qiu shang yi you de dan ge wang yuan jing zui da kou jing ye zhi you
yuan yuan bu gou yong
yi ge nan yi xiang xiang de da ke xue ji hua dan sheng le
yong fen bu quan qiu de
zu cheng yi ge kou jing ru di qiu zhi jing da xiao de xu ni wang yuan jing
qi suo da dao de ling min du he fen bian ben ling dou shi qian suo wei you de
tiao jian ke ke de guan ce dian
bao kuo xia wei yi he mo xi ge de huo shan
xi ban ya de nei hua da shan mai
zhi li de a ta ka ma sha mo
ming ke xue jia da cheng le
shi jian shi jie wang yuan jing
zhe yi zhong da guo ji he zuo ji hua
jue ding li yong shen zhang ji xian gan she ce liang ji shu
jiu shi li yong duo ge wei yu bu tong di fang de wang yuan jing zai tong yi shi jian jin xing lian he guan ce
zui hou jiang shu ju jin xing xiang guan xing fen xi zhi hou he bing
zhe yi ji shu zai she dian bo duan yi xiang dang cheng shu
zai zu jian da xing xu ni wang yuan jing de tong shi
ke xue jia men ye zai xun zhao zhao he shi de pai she mu biao
hei dong yin ying he zhou wei huan rao de xin yue ban guang huan fei chang xiao
zai pai zhao she bei neng li you xian di qing kuang xia
yao xiang pai she dao hei dong zhao pian
bi xu zhao dao yi ge kan qi lai jiao zhi jing zu gou da de hei dong zuo wei mu biao
ke xue jia men zhen xuan zhi hou
jue ding jiang jin lin de liang ge hei dong zuo wei zhu yao mu biao

de zhong xin hei dong
zhong xin de chao da zhi liang hei dong
you yu hei dong shi jian shi jie de da xiao yu qi zhi liang cheng zheng bi

qi shi jian shi jie yue da
wo men xuan ding de zhe liang ge hei dong zhi liang dou chao ji da

dan yao qing xi wei ta pai zhao
nan du hai shi ji qi da
* hei dong de zhi liang da yue xiang dang yu
suo dui ying de shi jie mian chi cun yue wei
ge tai yang de da xiao
wan guang nian zhi yao
zhe jiu yi wei zhe
ta ju da de shi jie mian zai wo men kan lai
da gai zhi you zhen jian na me xiao
jiu xiang wo men zhan zai di qiu shang qu guan kan yi ge fang zai yue qiu biao mian de cheng zi
zhong xin hei dong de zhi liang geng wei ju da
yi ge tai yang zhi liang
zhong xin hei dong yu di qiu de ju li yao bi
* yu di qiu zhi jian de ju li geng yuan
dan yin zhi liang pang da
suo yi ta de shi jian shi jie dui ke xue jia men er yan
* da xiao cha bu duo
shen zhi hai yao shao wei da yi dian
yao xiang kan qing chu liang ge hei dong shi jian shi jie de xi jie
shi jian shi jie wang yuan jing de kong jian fen bian lv yao da dao zu gou gao cai xing
bi ha bo wang yuan jing de fen bian lv gao chu
dan ye bie yi wei
zhi yao xu ni wang yuan jing zhen lie de fen bian lv zu gou gao
jiu yi ding neng cheng gong gei hei dong pai zhao
ru tong guan kan dian shi jie mu bi xu xuan dui pin dao yi yang
dui hei dong cheng xiang er yan
zai he shi de bo duan jin xing guan ce zhi guan zhong yao
ci qian de yi xi lie yan jiu biao ming
guan ce hei dong shi jian shi jie
de zui jia bo duan yue wei
zhe shi yin wei qi ti zai zhe ge bo duan de fu she zui ming liang
er qie she dian bo ye ke yi bu bei zu dang de cong yin he xi zhong xin chuan bo dao di qiu
zai zhe zhong qing kuang xia
wang yuan jing de fen bian lv qu jue yu wang yuan jing zhi jian de ju li
er fei dan ge wang yuan jing kou jing de da xiao
wei le zeng jia kong jian fen bian lv
yi kan qing geng wei xi xiao de qu yu
ke xue jia men zai ci ci jin xing guan ce de wang yuan jing zhen lie li zeng jia le wei yu zhi li he nan ji de wang yuan jing
zhe yang she zhi shi wei le yao bao zheng suo you
ge wang yuan jing dou neng kan dao zhe liang ge hei dong
cong er da dao zui gao de ling min du he zui da de kong jian fen bian lv
ge guan ce dian zu cheng de xu ni wang yuan jing wang luo
rang hei dong shou ci you le yi zhang
liu gei ke xue jia men de guan ce chuang kou qi fei chang duan zan
mei nian zhi you da yue
chu le guan ce shi jian shang de xian zhi

zhe yi wei zhe jiang shui hui gan rao guan ce
yao xiang shi jian shi jie wang yuan jing shun li guan ce

ji hua xuan ze de
ge wang yuan jing suo zai zhi chu jun hai ba jiao gao
jiang yu liang ji shao
quan bu qing tian de gai lv fei chang gao
yao cheng xiang cheng gong hai bi xu yao qiu suo you wang yuan jing zai shi jian shang wan quan tong bu

jiang shi xian tou xiang le yu zhou
zui hou de guan ce jie shu yu mei guo dong bu shi jian

zhe xie shu ju ci hou bei ji cheng yong yu huo de shi jian shi jie de tu xiang
wei le que bao xin hao de wen ding xing

dan ta men jiang shou ji da liang guan yu hei dong de shu ju xin xi

zai guan ce jie shu zhi hou

jing guo zhang da liang nian de

ye bu duan gong xian zhong guo zhi hui

gong ye hu lian wang tuo zhan

zhe yi ti wen bu dan yin fa le tan tao qian yan ke ji de lang chao
chan ye hu lian wang
yue gang ao da wan qu fa zhan gui hua gang yao
yao tui dong hu lian wang
ren gong zhi neng he shi ti jing ji shen du rong he

quan guo liang hui shang
gong ye hu lian wang you cheng wei re ci
zheng fu gong zuo bao gao li te bie ti dao
da zao gong ye hu lian wang ping tai
wei zhi zao ye zhuan xing sheng ji fu neng
lu xu liang xiang de zhong bang wen jian bu jin rang gong ye hu lian wang sheng wen
huan qing chu de shi fang zhe yi ge xin hao
yue gang ao da wan qu nai zhi quan guo
dou xi wang zai quan qiu xin yi lun ke ji yu chan ye ge ming zhong
tui dong ge ge chan ye jin xing
wang luo hua he zhi neng hua
de zhuan xing sheng ji
zhan ju quan qiu shu zi hua zhuan xing xian ji
zai gong ye hu lian wang ti xi zhong
wang luo shi ji chu
er biao zhi shi wang luo de ji chu
yao shi xian gong ye quan yao su
ge huan jie xin xi hu tong

quan guo ding ji jie dian zhi you
ge fen bie luo hu zai bei jing
wu han he chong qing

guang zhou zuo yong shen hou de chuan tong chan ye ji chu
su liao deng ru shu jia zhen
sui zhe hu lian wang ji shu de zai fa zhan

ke ji fa ju da de sheng chan li
gong ye hu lian wang de da ping tai jian she
li bu kai ge ge xiao ping tai
xiao jie dian de wan shan

xi guan de guang zhou
zao yi chu xian yi pi ju you jing zheng li de gong ye hu lian wang qi ye

zheng shi qi zhong zhi yi
qi chuang shi ren jian dong shi zhang ceng wan gui ye dui guang zhou fa zhan gong ye hu lian wang bao you hen da xin xin
wo men zuo wan zheng shi xuan bu le xin yi lun de rong zi
ceng wan gui gao su guang zhou ri bao quan mei ti ji zhe

bi zhan lve tou zi
zi ben miao zhun de shi yi ge ji dai kai tuo de shi chang
qi che hou shi chang
ju zhong jin zi ben fu zong cai huang bo jie shao
qi che hou shi chang gui mo yi da wan yi yuan ji
zai ru ci pang da de shi chang mian qian
ba tu lu que shi mu qian wei yi yi jia wei wei xiu chang ti gong yi zhan shi xin xi shou ji
yi zhan shi xian xia luo de fu wu de quan che jian jiao yi
ceng wan gui shi qi pei hang ye chu shen
shen zhi qi che pei jian jiao yi de tong dian
gong xu shuang fang yu yan bu tong
pei jian gong ying shang wei le guan li fang bian
hui you zi ji de yi tao pei jian bian hao guan li ti xi
dan ci qian mei you ren dui zhe xie bian hao ji zhong qi lai xing cheng biao zhun hua de shang pin
er xia you de qi che wei xiu chang ze shi yong
zai chuan tong de qi xiu mo shi li
wei xiu chang zhen zheng dong pei jian de ren hen shao
wei xiu ren yuan mian dui yi liang gu zhang de che
zhao chu gu zhang ling jian hou
ta zhi zhi dao ling jian da gai ming zi jiao shen me
bing bu zhi dao ta ju ti de bian hao
zhe jiu xu yao zhuan men de ren zai zhong jian bu ting gou tong yi que ding suo xu yao gou zhi de che jian

duo ji liu tong shang
dai li shang he pei jian zhi zao shang
zheng ge guo cheng zhong jian huan jie duo
geng yao ming de shi
bu tong de gong ying shang yong de shi bu tong de bian hao ti xi
tong yi ge pei jian hen ke neng bian hao ge bu xiang tong
er mu qian shi chang shang qi che pin pai fan duo
tong yi che xing hai you bu tong pei zhi
bu tong pei zhi you hui yin shen chu bu tong gui ge de pei jian
zhe zhong shang yi ji de pi pei guan xi
yin wei shang xia you zhi jian wu fa shun chang gou tong er dao zhi zheng ge qi pei shi chang hun luan bu kan
mou xie gong ying shang tong guo xin xi bu dui cheng shen zhi ke yi da cheng bao li de jiao yi
ba tu lu cong hun ju zhong sha chu
tong guo tong yi qi che pei jian bian ma
zheng he yi ge biao zhun hua
zhi neng hua de pei jian shu ju ku
zuo chu le gong xu shuang fang zhi jian de
ba tu lu qi pei pu

wei xiu chang zai zhe ge ping tai shang
ke yi tong guo wen zi miao shu
pai zhao shang chuan deng duo zhong fang shi jing zhun de zhao dao zi ji suo xu de pei jian

gong ying shang ze ke yi jiang pei jian fang jin ba tu lu de zhong xin cang ku

que yin ci huo de le ji yue hua

ti gong geng jing zhun
ge ren hua de zhi zao fu wu

zhi zao zheng ti fang an

zai lao pai qi ye an jing shi pin de liu shui xian shang
ge jian hua gong ren de wei zhi

yuan ben man tou jian hua cheng xu fei chang fan suo
gong ren shen zhe gong zuo fu
dai zhe mao zi he kou zhao

shou dong na qu tuo pan fang zai shen qian
xiao xin di yi bian shi yong jian dao yi bian zhuan dong man tou

ge gong ren de zhi neng man tou ji zheng zai gao su yun zhuan

geng bao zheng le shi pin wei sheng an quan
zhi neng man tou ji yi mei miao

wan dun leng dong shi pin

shou zhua bing fen jian ji

teng xun ye zai jin xing zhe fang mian de tan suo

ge yue cai neng shang gang
